There is a little traffic on the mountain on weekends. For the beautiful scenery, I will choose it next time I stay.

posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:Environment: The hotel is located in the Zhongshan Scenic Area, separated from the Ming Xiaoling Scenic Area by a wall. There is also a Diecui Lake in the north. There are long corridors connecting several buildings, and the scenery is beautiful. The hotel's mistaken scenic spot manual said that Zixia Lake Park is free. The front desk staff also said so and pointed the way. As a result, I went around a long circle but couldn't find the entrance. Later, I consulted the scenic area at the entrance of Ming Xiaoling No. 7 and learned that it has been included in the Ming Xiaoling Scenic Area. I had to buy a ticket and enter.

Facilities: The room is large, with a shower üöø and üõÅ. Although the furniture looks a bit old, it is still practical. The wardrobe at the corner is a bit small but fully equipped, and there is also a refrigerator. The family room has an additional 1.35m floor mat sofa bed, which is enough for 2 adults and 2 teenagers.

Service: Fruits were delivered every day, and the room service responded quickly. The biggest problem is the traffic control in the scenic area during holidays. Between 7 am and 7 pm, the hotel cannot be delivered by taxi or online car-hailing, and the interval between shuttle buses is too long. When I checked in for the first time, I fumbled for the shuttle bus in the East Parking Lot of Meihua Valley. I waited for half an hour and contacted the front desk several times before I saw the overloaded car full of people finally arrived. When I checked out later, I saw a long queue for the shuttle bus. Fortunately, there was not much luggage, so I took the luggage and walked directly outside the restricted area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe scenic area. It took about 20 minutes to walk past the Sifangcheng Shengong Shengde Monument and the pedestrian bridge where you can take pictures of the sycamore trees, which is also a scenic spot. If you stay in this hotel, don't arrange a trip outside the Zhongshan Scenic Area, otherwise it will be too inconvenient to enter and exit.

Catering: There is a Starbucks in the lobby. The hotel has a rich breakfast. Because there are no restaurants around, dinner is either takeout or solved in the restaurant on the first floor of the hotel. We didn't go to the buffet for dinner. We used the Dianping group purchase. The fish tasted delicious and the beef melted in the mouth. A la carte the next day is also acceptable. The price is a little expensive, but the taste is acceptable.
